\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00053}00053 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Data structure to store information about a certain "{}block"{} or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00054}00054 \textcolor{comment}{  /// sub-\/matrix from the overall matrix in the block preconditioning framework.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00055}00055 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00056}00056 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Example of use: Let's assume we want to form a concatenated matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00057}00057 \textcolor{comment}{  /// from the blocks of a Jacobian matrix that contains the following blocks:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00058}00058 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00059}00059 \textcolor{comment}{  /// [J\_00, J\_01, J\_02}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00060}00060 \textcolor{comment}{  ///  J\_10, J\_11, J\_12}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00061}00061 \textcolor{comment}{  ///  J\_20, J\_21, J\_22]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00062}00062 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00063}00063 \textcolor{comment}{  /// so that the new matrix has the entries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00064}00064 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00065}00065 \textcolor{comment}{  /// [ J\_01, J\_00}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00066}00066 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   J\_21,   0  ]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00067}00067 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00068}00068 \textcolor{comment}{  /// where "{}0"{} indicates zero matrix of the required size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00069}00069 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00070}00070 \textcolor{comment}{  /// To do this we create a 2x2 (the block size of the new concatenated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00071}00071 \textcolor{comment}{  /// matrix) VectorMatrix of BlockSelectors and then declare for each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00072}00072 \textcolor{comment}{  /// entry the block indices in the original matrix and if the entry}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00073}00073 \textcolor{comment}{  /// is to be included (and copied from the corresponding entry in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00074}00074 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the Jacobian (final boolean argument true) or if the block is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00075}00075 \textcolor{comment}{  /// to be omitted and replaced by an appropriately sized zero matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00076}00076 \textcolor{comment}{  /// For the example above this would be done as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00077}00077 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00078}00078 \textcolor{comment}{  /// VectorMatrix<BlockSelector> required\_block(2,2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00079}00079 \textcolor{comment}{  /// required\_block[0][0].select\_block(0,1,true);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00080}00080 \textcolor{comment}{  /// required\_block[0][1].select\_block(0,0,true);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00081}00081 \textcolor{comment}{  /// required\_block[1][0].select\_block(2,1,true);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00082}00082 \textcolor{comment}{  /// required\_block[1][1].select\_block(2,0,false);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00083}00083 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00084}00084 \textcolor{comment}{  /// and the concatenated matrix would then be built as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00085}00085 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00086}00086 \textcolor{comment}{  /// CRDoubleMatrix concatenated\_block1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00087}00087 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   = get\_concatenated\_block(required\_block);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00088}00088 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00089}00089 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Note that it is necessary to identify the row and column indices of any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00090}00090 \textcolor{comment}{  /// omitted blocks (here block J\_20 in the original matrix) to enable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00091}00091 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the correct setup of the sparse matrix storage.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00092}00092 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00093}00093 \textcolor{comment}{  /// The initial assignment of the boolean may be over-\/written with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00094}00094 \textcolor{comment}{  /// do\_not\_want\_block() member function; this can again be reversed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{  /// with the want\_block() counterpart. So if we call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00096}00096 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{  /// required\_block[0][0].do\_not\_want\_block();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{  /// and the build a new conctatenated matrix with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{  /// CRDoubleMatrix concatenated\_block2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   = get\_concatenated\_block(required\_block);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the resulting matrix would the anti-\/diagonal matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{  /// [   0  , J\_00}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   J\_21 ,   0  ]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Finally it is possible to specify a replacement block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{  /// by specifying a pointer to an appropriately sized matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{  /// that is to be used instead of the block in the Jacobian}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{  /// matrix, so if replacement\_block\_pt points to a matrix, R, say,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{  /// of the same size as J\_01, then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{  /// selected\_block[0][0].select\_block(0,1,true,replacement\_block\_pt);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{  /// then the resulting concatenated matrix would contain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{  /// [   R  , J\_00}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   J\_21 ,   0  ]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00374}00374 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Block Preconditioner base class. The block structure of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00375}00375 \textcolor{comment}{  /// overall problem is determined from the \(\backslash\)c Mesh's constituent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00376}00376 \textcolor{comment}{  /// elements. Each constituent element must be block-\/preconditionable -\/ i.e}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00377}00377 \textcolor{comment}{  /// must implement the \(\backslash\)c GeneralisedElements functions \(\backslash\)c ndof\_types() and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00378}00378 \textcolor{comment}{  /// get\_dof\_numbers\_for\_unknowns(...). A \(\backslash\)c Problem can have several}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00379}00379 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)c Meshes, but each \(\backslash\)c Mesh must contain elements with the same DOF types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00380}00380 \textcolor{comment}{  /// The association between global degrees of freedom and their unique local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00381}00381 \textcolor{comment}{  /// dof numbers is therefore based on information provided by the elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00382}00382 \textcolor{comment}{  /// We refer to the local dof numbers provided by the elements as the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00383}00383 \textcolor{comment}{  /// elemental dof numbers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00384}00384 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00385}00385 \textcolor{comment}{  /// By default each type of DOF is assumed to be unique type of block,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00386}00386 \textcolor{comment}{  /// but DOF types can be grouped together in a single block when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00387}00387 \textcolor{comment}{  /// block\_setup(...) is called.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00388}00388 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00389}00389 \textcolor{comment}{  /// This class can function in one of two ways. Either it acts as a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00390}00390 \textcolor{comment}{  /// stand-\/alone block preconditioner which computes and stores}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00391}00391 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the association between global degrees of freedom and their unique global}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00392}00392 \textcolor{comment}{  /// block numbers itself. Alternatively, the block preconditioner can act as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00393}00393 \textcolor{comment}{  /// a subsidiary block preconditioner within a (larger) master block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00394}00394 \textcolor{comment}{  /// preconditioner (pointed to by Master\_block\_preconditioner\_pt).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00395}00395 \textcolor{comment}{  /// The master block preconditioner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00396}00396 \textcolor{comment}{  /// must have an equal or greater number of block types. Examples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00397}00397 \textcolor{comment}{  /// are the FSI preconditioner which is the 3x3 "{}master block preconditioner"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00398}00398 \textcolor{comment}{  /// for the Navier-\/Stokes preconditioners which deals with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00399}00399 \textcolor{comment}{  /// 2x2 fluid-\/blocks within the overall structure. In this case, \(\backslash\)b only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00400}00400 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the master block preconditioner computes and stores the master}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00401}00401 \textcolor{comment}{  /// lookup schemes. All block preconditioners compute and store their own}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00402}00402 \textcolor{comment}{  /// optimised lookup schemes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00403}00403 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00404}00404 \textcolor{comment}{  /// In cases where a \(\backslash\)c Problem contains elements of different element types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00405}00405 \textcolor{comment}{  /// (e.g. fluid and solid elements in a fluid-\/structure interaction problem),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00406}00406 \textcolor{comment}{  /// access to the elements of the same type must be provided via pointers to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00407}00407 \textcolor{comment}{  /// (possibly auxiliary) \(\backslash\)c Meshes that only contain elements of a single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00408}00408 \textcolor{comment}{  /// type. The block preconditioner will then create global block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00409}00409 \textcolor{comment}{  /// numbers by concatenating the block types. Consider, e.g. a fluid-\/structure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00410}00410 \textcolor{comment}{  /// interaction problem in which the first \(\backslash\)c Mesh contains (fluid)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00411}00411 \textcolor{comment}{  /// elements whose degrees of freedom have been subdivided into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00412}00412 \textcolor{comment}{  /// types "{}0"{} (the velocity, say) and "{}1"{} (the pressure say), while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00413}00413 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the second \(\backslash\)c Mesh contains (solid) elements whose degrees of freedom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00414}00414 \textcolor{comment}{  /// are the nodal displacements, classified as its type "{}0"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00415}00415 \textcolor{comment}{  /// The combined block preconditioner then has three "{}block types"{}:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00416}00416 \textcolor{comment}{  /// "{}0"{}: Fluid velocity, "{}1"{}: Fluid pressure, "{}2"{}: Solid nodal positions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00417}00417 \textcolor{comment}{  /// NOTE: currently this preconditioner uses the same communicator as the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00418}00418 \textcolor{comment}{  /// underlying problem. We may need to change this in the future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00419}00419 \textcolor{comment}{}  \textcolor{comment}{//============================================================================}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00694}00694 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00695}00695       \textcolor{comment}{// The logic is this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00696}00696       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00697}00697       \textcolor{comment}{// Block\_to\_dof\_map\_coarse tells us which dof types belongs in each block.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00698}00698       \textcolor{comment}{// This is relative to this preconditioner, and describes the external}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00699}00699       \textcolor{comment}{// block and dof type mappings (what the preconditioner writer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00700}00700       \textcolor{comment}{// expects/sees).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00701}00701       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00702}00702       \textcolor{comment}{// As such, the dof types in Block\_to\_dof\_map\_coarse describes the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00703}00703       \textcolor{comment}{// dof-\/level blocks needed to be concatenated to produce block(i,j). These}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00704}00704       \textcolor{comment}{// dofs may have been coarsened.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00705}00705       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00706}00706       \textcolor{comment}{// Now, the dof blocks to concatenate comes from:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00707}00707       \textcolor{comment}{// If the dof block exists in Replacement\_dof\_block\_pt, then we make a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00708}00708       \textcolor{comment}{// deep copy of it. Otherwise, if this is the upper-\/most master block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00709}00709       \textcolor{comment}{// preconditioner then we get it from the original matrix via function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00710}00710       \textcolor{comment}{// internal\_get\_block(...) otherwise, if this is a subsidiary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00711}00711       \textcolor{comment}{// block preconditioner, we go one level up the hierarchy and repeat the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00712}00712       \textcolor{comment}{// process.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00713}00713       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00714}00714       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00715}00715       \textcolor{comment}{// A small note about indirections which caused me some headache.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00716}00716       \textcolor{comment}{// Thought I would mention it here in case the below code needs to be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00717}00717       \textcolor{comment}{// re-\/visited.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00718}00718       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00719}00719       \textcolor{comment}{// A small subtlety with indirections:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00720}00720       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00721}00721       \textcolor{comment}{// The underlying ordering of the dof-\/level blocks is STILL AND ALWAYS the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00722}00722       \textcolor{comment}{// `natural' ordering determined by first the elements then the order of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00723}00723       \textcolor{comment}{// the meshes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00724}00724       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00725}00725       \textcolor{comment}{// But during the process of block\_setup(...), the external (perceived)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00726}00726       \textcolor{comment}{// block ordering may have changed. So some indirection has to take place,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00727}00727       \textcolor{comment}{// this mapping is maintained in Block\_to\_dof\_map\_coarse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00728}00728       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00729}00729       \textcolor{comment}{// For example, take the Lagrangian preconditioner, which expects the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00730}00730       \textcolor{comment}{// natural dof type ordering:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00731}00731       \textcolor{comment}{// 0 1 2 3  4  5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00732}00732       \textcolor{comment}{// u v p uc vc L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00733}00733       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00734}00734       \textcolor{comment}{// If the mapping given to block\_setup(...) is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00735}00735       \textcolor{comment}{// dof\_to\_block\_map = [0, 1, 4, 2, 3, 5]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00736}00736       \textcolor{comment}{// saying that: dof type 0 goes to block 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00737}00737       \textcolor{comment}{//              dof type 1 goes to block 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00738}00738       \textcolor{comment}{//              dof type 2 goes to block 4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00739}00739       \textcolor{comment}{//              dof type 3 goes to block 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00740}00740       \textcolor{comment}{//              dof type 4 goes to block 3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00741}00741       \textcolor{comment}{//              dof type 5 goes to block 5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00742}00742       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00743}00743       \textcolor{comment}{// The function block\_setup(...) will populate the vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00744}00744       \textcolor{comment}{// Block\_to\_dof\_map\_coarse with [[0][1][3][4][2][5]],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00745}00745       \textcolor{comment}{// which says that get\_block(0,0) will get the u block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00746}00746       \textcolor{comment}{//                 get\_block(1,1) will get the v block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00747}00747       \textcolor{comment}{//                 get\_block(2,2) will get the uc block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00748}00748       \textcolor{comment}{//                 get\_block(3,3) will get the vc block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00749}00749       \textcolor{comment}{//                 get\_block(4,4) will get the p block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00750}00750       \textcolor{comment}{//                 get\_block(5,5) will get the L block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00751}00751       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00752}00752       \textcolor{comment}{// i.e. the ordering of the block types is a permutation of the dof types,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00753}00753       \textcolor{comment}{// so that we now have the following block ordering:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00754}00754       \textcolor{comment}{// 0 1 2  3  4 5 <-\/ block ordering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00755}00755       \textcolor{comment}{// u v uc vc p L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00756}00756       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00757}00757       \textcolor{comment}{// Now, the writer expects to work with the block ordering. I.e. when we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00758}00758       \textcolor{comment}{// replace a dof-\/level block, say the pressure block, we call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00759}00759       \textcolor{comment}{// set\_replacement\_dof\_block(4,4,Matrix);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00760}00760       \textcolor{comment}{// Similarly, when we want the pressure block, we call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00761}00761       \textcolor{comment}{// get\_block(4,4);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00762}00762       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00763}00763       \textcolor{comment}{// Now, the below code uses the indirection maintained in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00764}00764       \textcolor{comment}{// Block\_to\_dof\_map\_coarse. I.e. When we call get\_block(4,4), we use the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00765}00765       \textcolor{comment}{// mapping Block\_to\_dof\_map\_coarse[4] = 2, we get the block (2,2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00766}00766       \textcolor{comment}{// (from Replacement\_dof\_block\_pt or internal\_get\_block), since the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00767}00767       \textcolor{comment}{// underlying dof\_to\_block mapping is still the identity, i.e. it has not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00768}00768       \textcolor{comment}{// changed from:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00769}00769       \textcolor{comment}{// 0 1 2 3  4  5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00770}00770       \textcolor{comment}{// u v p uc vc L}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00771}00771       \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00772}00772       \textcolor{comment}{// So, block (4,4) (pressure block) maps to the block (2,2).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00773}00773 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00774}00774       \textcolor{comment}{// How many external dof types are in this block?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00775}00775       \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} ndofblock\_in\_row = \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1BlockPreconditioner_ae047d81b8179dfd09b70cf35f40f62ca}{Block\_to\_dof\_map\_coarse}}[\mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_adb50e893b86b3e55e751a42eab3cba82}{i}}].size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00776}00776       \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} ndofblock\_in\_col = \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1BlockPreconditioner_ae047d81b8179dfd09b70cf35f40f62ca}{Block\_to\_dof\_map\_coarse}}[j].size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00777}00777 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00778}00778       \textcolor{comment}{// If there is only one dof block in this block then there is no need to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00780}00780       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ndofblock\_in\_row == 1 \&\& ndofblock\_in\_col == 1)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00871}00871 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00872}00872         \textcolor{comment}{// Concatenation of matrices require the distribution of the individual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00873}00873         \textcolor{comment}{// sub-\/matrices (for both row and column). This is because concatenation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00874}00874         \textcolor{comment}{// is implemented without communication in such a way that the rows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00875}00875         \textcolor{comment}{// and column values are both permuted, the permutation is defined by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00876}00876         \textcolor{comment}{// the individual distributions of the sub blocks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00877}00877         \textcolor{comment}{// Without a vector of distributions describing the distributions of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00878}00878         \textcolor{comment}{// of the rows, we do not know how to permute the rows. For the columns,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00879}00879         \textcolor{comment}{// although CRDoubleMatrices does not have a column distribution, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00880}00880         \textcolor{comment}{// concatenated matrix must have it's columns permuted, so we mirror}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00881}00881         \textcolor{comment}{// the diagonal and get the corresponding row distribution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00882}00882         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00883}00883         \textcolor{comment}{// Confused? -\/ Example: Say we have a matrix with dof blocking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00884}00884         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00885}00885         \textcolor{comment}{//   | a | b | c | d | e |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00886}00886         \textcolor{comment}{// -\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00887}00887         \textcolor{comment}{// a |   |   |   |   |   |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00888}00888         \textcolor{comment}{// -\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00889}00889         \textcolor{comment}{// b |   |   |   |   |   |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00890}00890         \textcolor{comment}{// -\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l00891}00891         \textcolor{comment}{// c |   |   |   |   |   |}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l01441}01441       \textcolor{comment}{// minimise this process by creating it once, then store a key to the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{block__preconditioner_8h_source_l01443}01443       \textcolor{comment}{// is already a key in Auxiliary\_block\_distribution\_pt, if it is in there,}}
